They become so accustomed to this state that they find slower-paced activities aversive. They push their nervous system to its limits, crash, then push to the limits again. Parents need to slow things down with them. Find shared calming activities \u2014 like going for a walk, listening to music, baking \u2014 where the reward is being in this state together. They become so accustomed to this state that they find slower-paced activities aversive. They push their nervous system to its limits, crash, then push to the limits again. Parents need to slow things down with them. Find shared calming activities \u2014 like going for a walk, listening to music, baking \u2014 where the reward is being in this state together.
